PART IV (B) – GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA – 30.08.2011
1 A
1A
NOTICE  OF  POLL
Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262)
NOTICE  UNDER  SECTION  38(1)
ELECTION OF MAYOR, DEPUTY MAYOR AND MEMBERS OF THE COLOMBO MUNICIPAL COUNCIL
NOTICE is hereby given under section 38(1) of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance that the above Election is contested
and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a.m. and 4.00 p.m. on 08th October, 2011 and that —
(a) the single list containing the names of the Candidates as indicated by the Candidates but placed in alphabetical
order in Sinhala of each Recognized Political Party and each Independent Group of  Election as Mayor,
Deputy Mayor and as Members of the above mentioned Local Authority, the serial number assigned to each
such Candidate and the approved symbol allotted to each such Party and each such Independent Group and
the distinguishing number allotted to each such Independent Group ; and
(b) the situation of the Polling Station or Stations for each of the Polling Districts in the above mentioned
Electoral Area and the particular Polling Station reserved for female votes,
are as specified in the Schedule below.
2. The order in which the name of each Recognized Political Party  and the distinguishing number of each Independent
Group appearing in the Schedule below is the same order in which these particulars will be printed on the ballot paper.
A. S
ENANAYAKE,
Returning Officer,
Colombo Municipal Council,
Assistant Returning Officer,
Administrative District of Colombo.
Elections Office,
Colombo District.
30th August, 2011.
EXTRAORDINARY
The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka

Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262)
NOTICE  UNDER  SECTION  38(1)
ELECTION OF MAYOR, DEPUTY MAYOR AND MEMBERS OF THE SRI JAYAWARDHANAPURA KOTTE MUNICIPAL COUNCIL
NOTICE is hereby given under Section 38(1) of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance that the above Election is contested
and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a.m. and 4.00 p.m. on 08th October, 2011 and that —
(a) the single list containing the names of the Candidates as indicated by the Candidates but placed in alphabetical
order in Sinhala of each Recognized Political Party and each Independent Group for Election as Mayor,
Deputy Mayor and as Members of the above mentioned Local Authority, the serial number assigned to each
such Candidate and the approved symbol allotted to each such Party and each such Independent Group and
the distinguishing number allotted to each such Independent Group ; and
(b) the situation of the Polling Station or Stations for each of the Polling Districts in the above mentioned
Electoral Area, and the Particular Polling Stations reserved for female voters
are as specified in the Schedule below.
2. The order in which the name of each Recognized Political Party  and the distinguishing number of each Independent
Group appearing in the Schedule below is the same order in which these particulars will be printed on the ballot paper.

NOTICE  UNDER  SECTION 38(1)
ELECTION  OF M AYOR, DEPUTY M AYOR AND MEMBERS OF THE M ORATUW A M UNICIPAL COUNCIL
NOTICE is hereby given under Section 38(1) of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance that the above Election is contested
and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a. m. and 4.00 p. m. on 08th October, 2011 and that –
(a) the single list containing the names of the Candidates as indicated by the Candidates but placed in alphabetical
order in Sinhala of each Recognized Political Party and each Independent Group of  Election as Mayor, Deputy
Mayor and as Members of the above mentioned Local Authority, the serial number assigned to each such
Candidate and the approved symbol allotted to each such Party and each such Independent Group and the
distinguishing number allotted to each such Independent Group ; and
(b) the situation of the Polling Station or Stations for each of the Polling Districts in the above mentioned Electoral
Area, and the particular Polling Stations reserved for female voters,
are as specified in the Schedule below.
2. The order in which the name of each Recognized Political Party and the distinguishing number of each Independent
Group appearing in the Schedule below is the same order in which these particulars will be printed on the ballot paper.

NOTICE   OF   POLL
Local  Authorities  Elections  Ordinance  (Chapter  262)
NOTICE  UNDER  SECTION 38(1)
ELECTION  OF CHAIRMAN, VICE CHAIRMAN AND MEMBERS OF THE KOLONNAW A URBAN COUNCIL
NOTICE is hereby given under Section 38(1) of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance that the above Election is contested
and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a. m. and 4.00 p. m. on 08th October, 2011 and that –
(a) the single list containing the names of the Candidates as indicated by the Candidates but placed in alphabetical
order in Sinhala of each Recognized Political Party and each Independent Group for Election as Chairman, Vice
Chairman and as Members of the above mentioned Local Authority, the serial number assigned to each such
Candidate and the approved symbol allotted to each such Party and each such Independent Group and the
distinguishing number allotted to each such Independent Group ; and
(b) the situation of the Polling Station or Stations for each of the Polling Districts in the above mentioned Electoral
Area, and the particular Polling Stations reserved for female voters,
are as specified in the Schedule below.
2. The order in which the name of each Recognized Political Party and the distinguishing number of each Independent
Group appearing in the Schedule below is the same order in which these particulars will be printed on the ballot paper.
J. A. S. P . J
AY ASINGHE,

NOTICE is hereby given under Section 38(1) of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance that the above Election is contested
and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a.m. and 4.00 p.m. on 08th October, 2011 and that —

NOTICE  UNDER  SECTION 38(1)
ELECTION  OF MAYOR, DEPUTY MAYOR AND MEMBERS OF THE MATARA MUNICIPAL COUNCIL
NOTICE is hereby given under Section 38(1) of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance that the above Election is contested
and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a. m. and 4.00 p. m. on 08th October, 2011 and that –
(a) the single list containing the names of the Candidates as indicated by the Candidates but placed in alphabetical
order in Sinhala of each Recognized Political Party and each Independent Group for Election as  Mayor, Deputy
Mayor  and as Members of the above mentioned Local Authority, the serial number assigned to each such
Candidate and  the approved symbol allotted to each such Party and  each such  Independent Group and the
distinguishing number allotted to each such Independent Group ; and
(b) the situation of the Polling Station or Stations for each of the Polling Districts in the above mentioned Electoral
Area, and the  particular Polling  Stations reserved  for female voters
are as specified in the Schedule below.
2. The order in which the name of each Recognized Political Party and the distinguishing number of each Independent
Group appearing in the Schedule below is the same order in which these particulars will be printed on the ballot paper.
